TITLE      Neutron capture cross section measurement of 129I and  2361500100003 
           127I using the NaI(Tl) spectrometer of the ANNRI       2361500100004 
           beamline at J-PARC                                     2361500100005 
AUTHOR     (G.Rovira,A.Kimura,S.Nakamura,S.Endo,O.Iwamoto,        2361500100006 
           N.Iwamoto, Y.Toh,M.Segawa,M.Maeda,T.Katabuchi)         2361500100007 
INSTITUTE  (2JPNJAE,2JPNTIT)                                      2361500100008 
REFERENCE  (J,EPJ/A,60,120,2024)                                  2361500100009 
           #doi:10.1140/epja/s10050-024-01333-3                   2361500100010 
REL-REF    (I,,K.Kino+,J,NIM/A,736,66,2014)                       2361500100011 
           Energy resolution of the pulsed neutron was given.     2361500100012 
FACILITY   (SYNCH,2JPNJAE) ANNRI(BL04) beam line of MLF at J-PARC 2361500100013 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) Spallation reaction in a mercury target        2361500100014 
           irradiated with 3-GeV protons (800 kW) .               2361500100015 
           The proton beams were supplied at a repetition rate of 2361500100016 
           25 Hz and in the "double-bunch mode", in which         2361500100017 
           the pulsed protons consist of two bunches, each with   2361500100018 
           a width of 100 ns, at intervals of 600 ns.             2361500100019 
           Produced neutrons were slowed down in a supercritical  2361500100020 
           para hydrogen moderator.                               2361500100021 
           Disk chopper with a semicircular shape was used to cut 2361500100022 
           the low-energy tail of neutron pulse.                  2361500100023 
           The experiments were performed using the 7-mm          2361500100024 
           collimator.                                            2361500100025 
INC-SPECT  The neutron spectrum was reconstructed using the 478   2361500100026 
           keV gamma-rays from gamma rays from 10B(n,alpha        2361500100027 
           gamma) 7Li reaction.                                   2361500100028 
DETECTOR   (NAICR)                                                2361500100029 
            -Size: 330 mm (diam.) and 203 mm in thickness         2361500100030 
            -Angle: 90 deg with respect to the neutron beam line  2361500100031 
            -Flight length: 27.9 m                                2361500100032 
            -DAQ: CAEN V1720 Digitizer (12bit, 250MHz)            2361500100033 
SAMPLE     127I Sample: A Na127I compressed pellet with mass of   2361500100034 
           562 +- 1 mg.                                           2361500100035 
             Area density: 127I (7.18 +- 0.02 ) x10E-4 at/b       2361500100036 
           129I sample: A NaI pellet with a mass of 404 +- 1 mg   2361500100037 
            and activity of 2.65 MBq, shielded in a Ti case.      2361500100038 
           The sample contained 129I with an isotopic             2361500100039 
           abundance of 85.9%, together with 14.1% of 127I as an  2361500100040 
           impurity.                                              2361500100041 
             Area density: 127I (0.99 +- 0.01) x10E-4 at/b        2361500100042 
                           129I (6.00 +- 0.02) x10E-4 at/b        2361500100043

METHOD     (TOF,PHWT)                                             2361500200004 
ANALYSIS   Measurements with the carbon sample and                2361500200005 
           "Blank (no sample) " were used for background          2361500200006 
           estimation. The weighting function was normalized by   2361500200007 
           comparing the experimental results of the Au sample    2361500200008 
           at the 1st resonance using the saturated resonance     2361500200009 
           method.                                                2361500200010 
CORRECTION The dead-time correction was applied with the          2361500200011 
           extended dead-time model. Correction factors for       2361500200012 
           self-shielding and multiple scattering effects were    2361500200013 
           deduced using the Monte-Carlo simulation code PHITS.   2361500200014

           (ERR-2) Unc. due to deadtime correction                2361500200018

ANALYSIS   Measurements with the carbon sample,                   2361500500005 
           "Blank (no sample) ", and "Dummy case with Na127I"     2361500500006 
           were used for background estimation.                   2361500500007 
           The sample contained 14.1% of 127I as an impurity.     2361500500008 
           The neutron capture cross section for 129I was         2361500500009 
           normalized to the results of 127I in 23615003,         2361500500010 
           at four large resonances of 127I, with considering     2361500500011 
           the isotopic abundance of 127I.                        2361500500012 
           The influence of 127I in the sample was not subtracted.2361500500013 
           The presented data is sum of capture cross section of  2361500500014 
           129I (85.9%) and that of 127I (14.1%) .                2361500500015

           extended dead-time model.                              2361500500017 
           Correction factors for self-shielding and multiple     2361500500018 
           scattering effects for the 129 sample and the dummy    2361500500019 
           case were deduced using the Monte-Carlo simulation     2361500500020 
           code PHITS.                                            2361500500021
